  <hr> 
  <a name="Auto Login"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Auto Login</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited class names that implement com.liferay.portal.security.auth.AutoLogin. These classes will run in consecutive order for all unauthenticated users until one of them return a valid user id and password combination. If no valid combination is returned, then the request continues to process normally. If a valid combination is returned, then the portal will automatically login that user with the returned user id and password combination. </p> 
  <p>For example, com.liferay.portal.security.auth.RememberMeAutoLogin reads from a cookie to automatically log in a user who previously logged in while checking on the "Remember Me" box. </p> 
  <p>This interface allows deployers to easily configure the portal to work with other SSO servers. See com.liferay.portal.security.auth.CASAutoLogin for an example of how to configure the portal with Yale's SSO server. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    auto.login.hooks=com.liferay.portal.security.auth.CASAutoLogin,com.liferay.portal.security.auth.FacebookAutoLogin,com.liferay.portal.security.auth.NtlmAutoLogin,com.liferay.portal.security.auth.OpenIdAutoLogin,com.liferay.portal.security.auth.OpenSSOAutoLogin,com.liferay.portal.security.auth.RememberMeAutoLogin,com.liferay.portal.security.auth.SiteMinderAutoLogin
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the hosts that will be ignored for auto login. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    auto.login.ignore.hosts=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the paths that will be ignored for auto login. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    auto.login.ignore.paths=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="SSO with MAC (Message Authentication Code)"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>SSO with MAC (Message Authentication Code)</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>To use SSO with MAC, post to an URL like: </p> 
  <p></p>
  <pre>     http://localhost:8080/c/portal/login?cmd=already-registered&amp;login=
   <userid|emailaddress>
    &amp;password=
    <mac> 
    </mac>
   </userid|emailaddress></pre>
  <p></p> 
  <p>Pass the MAC in the password field. Make sure the MAC gets URL encoded because it might contain characters not allowed in a URL. </p> 
  <p>SSO with MAC also requires that you set the following property in system.properties: </p> 
  <p></p>
  <pre>     com.liferay.util.servlet.SessionParameters=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <p>See the following links: </p> 
  <p></p>
  <pre>     http://issues.liferay.com/browse/LEP-1288
     http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Message_authentication_code
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable SSO with MAC. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    auth.mac.allow=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the algorithm to use for MAC encryption. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    auth.mac.algorithm=MD5
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the shared key used to generate the MAC. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    auth.mac.shared.key=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Passwords"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Passwords</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the following encryption algorithm to encrypt passwords. The default algorithm is SHA (SHA-1). If set to NONE, passwords are stored in the database as plain text. The SHA-512 algorithm is currently unsupported. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    passwords.encryption.algorithm=SHA
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    passwords.encryption.algorithm=BCRYPT
    passwords.encryption.algorithm=UFC-CRYPT
    passwords.encryption.algorithm=MD2
    passwords.encryption.algorithm=MD5
    passwords.encryption.algorithm=NONE
    passwords.encryption.algorithm=SHA-256
    passwords.encryption.algorithm=SHA-384
    passwords.encryption.algorithm=SSHA
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Digested passwords are encoded via base64 or hex encoding. The default is base64. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    passwords.digest.encoding=base64
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    passwords.digest.encoding=hex
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a class name that implements com.liferay.portal.security.pwd.Toolkit. This class will be called to generate and validate passwords. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    passwords.toolkit=com.liferay.portal.security.pwd.PasswordPolicyToolkit
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    passwords.toolkit=com.liferay.portal.security.pwd.RegExpToolkit
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>If you choose to use com.liferay.portal.security.pwd.PasswordPolicyToolkit as your password toolkit, you can choose either static or dynamic password generation. Static is set through the property "passwords.passwordpolicytoolkit.static" and dynamic uses the class com.liferay.util.PwdGenerator to generate the password. If you are using LDAP password syntax checking, you will also have to use the static generator so that you can guarantee that passwords obey its rules. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    passwords.passwordpolicytoolkit.generator=dynamic
    passwords.passwordpolicytoolkit.static=iheartliferay
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    passwords.passwordpolicytoolkit.generator=static
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the character sets for password validation. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    passwords.passwordpolicytoolkit.charset.lowercase=abcdefghjkmnpqrstuvwxyz
    passwords.passwordpolicytoolkit.charset.numbers=0123456789
    passwords.passwordpolicytoolkit.charset.symbols=_.!@$*=-?
    passwords.passwordpolicytoolkit.charset.uppercase=ABCDEFGHJKLMNPQRSTUVWXYZ
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>If you choose to use com.liferay.portal.security.pwd.RegExpToolkit as your password toolkit, set the regular expression pattern that will be used to generate and validate passwords. </p> 
  <p>Note that \ is replaced with \\ to work in Java. </p> 
  <p>The first pattern ensures that passwords must have at least 4 valid characters consisting of digits or letters. </p> 
  <p>The second pattern ensures that passwords must have at least 8 valid characters consisting of digits or letters. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    passwords.regexptoolkit.pattern=(?=.{4})(?:[a-zA-Z0-9]*)
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    passwords.regexptoolkit.pattern=(?=.{8})(?:[a-zA-Z0-9]*)
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the length and key for generating passwords. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    passwords.regexptoolkit.charset=0123456789ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz
    passwords.regexptoolkit.length=8
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    passwords.regexptoolkit.charset=0123456789
    passwords.regexptoolkit.length=4
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the name of the default password policy. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    passwords.default.policy.name=Default Password Policy
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Permissions"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Permissions</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the default permission checker class used by com.liferay.portal.security.permission.PermissionCheckerFactory to check permissions for actions on objects. This class can be overriden with a custom class that implements com.liferay.portal.security.permission.PermissionChecker. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.checker=com.liferay.portal.security.permission.AdvancedPermissionChecker
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    permissions.checker=com.liferay.portal.security.permission.SimplePermissionChecker
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the algorithm used to check permissions for a user. This is useful so that you can optimize the search for different databases. See com.liferay.portal.service.impl.PermissionLocalServiceImpl. </p> 
  <p>Algorithms 1 through 4 are essentially the same but make calls in different orders depending on how the database is optimized and how the portal permissions are used. Algorithm 5 moves to a completely role based permissions check for better performance. Permissions by users are no longer supported, yet it uses the same table structure as algorithms 1-4. </p> 
  <p>Algorithm 6 is the current algorithm for Liferay 6 and above. It supports role based permissions like algorithm 5, but does so by using only one table and bitwise operations. This makes it perform far better than the other algorithms. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.user.check.algorithm=6
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    permissions.user.check.algorithm=1
    permissions.user.check.algorithm=2
    permissions.user.check.algorithm=3
    permissions.user.check.algorithm=4
    permissions.user.check.algorithm=5
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the default permissions list filter class. This class must implement com.liferay.portal.kernel.security.permission.PermissionsListFilter. This is used if you want to filter the list of permissions before it is actually persisted. For example, if you want to make sure that all users who create objects never have the UPDATE action, then you can filter that list and remove any permissions that have the UPDATE action before it is persisted. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.list.filter=com.liferay.portal.security.permission.PermissionsListFilterImpl
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to configure permission caching to block. See the property "ehcache.blocking.cache.allowed" for more information. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.object.blocking.cache=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Configure this threshold to indicate when to use the custom SQL finder to check resource permissions. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.role.resource.permission.query.threshold=10
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>The permissions cache uses a thread local map to store the most frequently accessed items to lower the number of queries to the underlying cache. Set the maximum map size to 0 to disable the thread level cache. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.thread.local.cache.max.size=100
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable inline SQL permission checks. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.inline.sql.check.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Configure this threshold to indicate when to pass in the resource block IDs directly to the inlinbe SQL statement and when to use a subselect to determine the resource block IDS. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.inline.sql.resource.block.query.threshhold=100
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to use permission checking when reading custom attributes by default. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.custom.attribute.read.check.by.default=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to use permission checking when writing custom attributes by default. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.custom.attribute.write.check.by.default=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the following to true to automatically check the view permission on parent categories or folders when checking the permission on an specific item. </p> 
  <p>For example, if set to true, to be able to have access to a document, a user must have the view permission on the document's folder and all its parent folders. Or, to have access to a comment, a user must have the view permission on the comments's category and all its parent categories. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.view.dynamic.inheritance=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the following to true to enable propagation of permissions between models. </p> 
  <p>For example, when setting the permissions on a a specific Wiki node, if you assign a role a permission (e.g. DELETE), then the assignment of that permission is also propagated to all Wiki pages that belong to that Wiki node. </p> 
  <p>The actual logic of how permissions are propagated among models is specified per portlet. See liferay-portlet.xml's use of the element "permission-propagator". </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.propagation.enabled=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if resources should assume that all users have the Guest role. Set this to false if resources will not assume that all users have the Guest role and thus do not automatically inherit permissions that belong to the Guest role. </p> 
  <p>Setting this property to false may require users to grant permissions to roles like Site Member and User. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    permissions.check.guest.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Captcha"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Captcha</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the maximum number of captcha checks per portlet session. Set this value to 0 to always check. Set this value to a number less than 0 to never check. Unauthenticated users will always be checked on every request if captcha checks is enabled. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    captcha.max.challenges=1
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set whether or not to use captcha checks for the following actions. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    captcha.check.portal.create_account=true
    captcha.check.portal.send_password=true
    captcha.check.portlet.message_boards.edit_category=false
    captcha.check.portlet.message_boards.edit_message=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the engine used to generate captchas. reCAPTCHA uses an external service that must be configured independently but provides an audible alternative which makes the captcha accessible to the visually impaired. See https://www.google.com/recaptcha/admin/create for details. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    captcha.engine.impl=com.liferay.portal.captcha.simplecaptcha.SimpleCaptchaImpl
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    captcha.engine.impl=com.liferay.portal.captcha.recaptcha.ReCaptchaImpl
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>reCAPTCHA </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    captcha.engine.recaptcha.key.private=
    captcha.engine.recaptcha.key.public=
    captcha.engine.recaptcha.url.script=http://www.google.com/recaptcha/api/challenge?k=
    captcha.engine.recaptcha.url.noscript=http://www.google.com/recaptcha/api/noscript?k=
    captcha.engine.recaptcha.url.verify=http://www.google.com/recaptcha/api/verify
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>SimpleCaptcha </p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the height and width for captcha images generated by SimpleCaptcha. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    captcha.engine.simplecaptcha.height=50
    captcha.engine.simplecaptcha.width=150
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited class names that implement nl.captcha.backgrounds.BackgroundProducer. These classes will be randomly used by SimpleCaptcha to generate a background for a captcha image. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    captcha.engine.simplecaptcha.background.producers=nl.captcha.backgrounds.FlatColorBackgroundProducer,nl.captcha.backgrounds.GradiatedBackgroundProducer,nl.captcha.backgrounds.SquigglesBackgroundProducer,nl.captcha.backgrounds.TransparentBackgroundProducer
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited class names that implement nl.captcha.gimpy.GimpyRenderer. These classes will be randomly used by SimpleCaptcha to gimp a captcha image. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    captcha.engine.simplecaptcha.gimpy.renderers=nl.captcha.gimpy.BlockGimpyRenderer,nl.captcha.gimpy.DropShadowGimpyRenderer,nl.captcha.gimpy.FishEyeGimpyRenderer,nl.captcha.gimpy.RippleGimpyRenderer,nl.captcha.gimpy.ShearGimpyRenderer
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    captcha.engine.simplecaptcha.gimpy.renderers=nl.captcha.gimpy.RippleGimpyRenderer
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited class names that implement nl.captcha.noise.NoiseProducer. These classes will be randomly used by SimpleCaptcha to add noise to a captcha image. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    captcha.engine.simplecaptcha.noise.producers=nl.captcha.noise.CurvedLineNoiseProducer,nl.captcha.noise.StraightLineNoiseProducer
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    captcha.engine.simplecaptcha.noise.producers=nl.captcha.noise.CurvedLineNoiseProducer
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited class names that implement nl.captcha.text.producer.TextProducer. These classes will be randomly used by SimpleCaptcha to generate text for a captcha image. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    captcha.engine.simplecaptcha.text.producers=com.liferay.portal.captcha.simplecaptcha.PinNumberTextProducer
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    captcha.engine.simplecaptcha.text.producers=com.liferay.portal.captcha.simplecaptcha.DictionaryWordTextProducer,com.liferay.portal.captcha.simplecaptcha.PinNumberTextProducer,nl.captcha.text.producer.DefaultTextProducer,nl.captcha.text.producer.FiveLetterFirstNameTextProducer
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited class names that implement nl.captcha.text.renderer .WordRenderer. These classes will be randomly used by SimpleCaptcha to render text for a captcha image. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    captcha.engine.simplecaptcha.word.renderers=nl.captcha.text.renderer.DefaultWordRenderer
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    captcha.engine.simplecaptcha.word.renderers=nl.captcha.text.renderer.ColoredEdgesWordRenderer,nl.captcha.text.renderer.DefaultWordRenderer
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Startup Events"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Startup Events</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited class names that extend com.liferay.portal.struts.SimpleAction. These classes will run at the specified event. </p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Global startup event that runs once when the portal initializes. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    global.startup.events=com.liferay.portal.events.GlobalStartupAction,com.liferay.portal.events.CryptoStartupAction
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Application startup event that runs once for every web site instance of the portal that initializes. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    application.startup.events=com.liferay.portal.events.AddDefaultDataAction,com.liferay.portal.events.AppStartupAction,com.liferay.portal.events.ChannelHubAppStartupAction
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    application.startup.events=com.liferay.portal.events.AppStartupAction,com.liferay.portal.events.SampleAppStartupAction
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Shutdown Events"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Shutdown Events</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited class names that extend com.liferay.portal.struts.SimpleAction. These classes will run at the specified event. </p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Global shutdown event that runs once when the portal shuts down. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    global.shutdown.events=com.liferay.portal.events.GlobalShutdownAction
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Application shutdown event that runs once for every web site instance of the portal that shuts down. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    application.shutdown.events=com.liferay.portal.events.AppShutdownAction,com.liferay.portal.events.ChannelHubAppShutdownAction
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Programmatically kill the Java process on shutdown. This is a workaround for a bug in Tomcat and Linux where the process hangs on forever. </p> 
  <p>See http://issues.liferay.com/browse/LEP-2048 for more information. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    shutdown.programmatically.exit=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Portal Events"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Portal Events</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited class names that extend com.liferay.portal.kernel.events.Action. These classes will run before or after the specified event. </p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Servlet service event (the pre-service events have an associated error page and will forward to that page if an exception is thrown during excecution of the events). The pre-service events process before Struts processes the request. The post-service events process after Struts processes the request. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    servlet.service.events.pre=com.liferay.portal.events.ServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.DeviceServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.ThemeServicePreAction
    servlet.service.events.pre.error.page=/common/error.jsp
    servlet.service.events.post=com.liferay.portal.events.ServicePostAction
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    servlet.service.events.pre=com.liferay.portal.events.LogMemoryUsageAction,com.liferay.portal.events.LogThreadCountAction,com.liferay.portal.events.ServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.DeviceServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.ThemeServicePreAction
    servlet.service.events.pre=com.liferay.portal.events.LogSessionIdAction,com.liferay.portal.events.ServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.DeviceServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.ThemeServicePreAction
    servlet.service.events.pre=com.liferay.portal.events.ServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.DeviceServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.ThemeServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.RandomLayoutAction
    servlet.service.events.pre=com.liferay.portal.events.ServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.DeviceServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.ThemeServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.RandomLookAndFeelAction
    servlet.service.events.pre=com.liferay.portal.events.ServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.DeviceServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.ThemeServicePreAction,com.liferay.portal.events.SecureRequestAction
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Login event </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    login.events.pre=com.liferay.portal.events.LoginPreAction
    login.events.post=com.liferay.portal.events.ChannelLoginPostAction,com.liferay.portal.events.DefaultLandingPageAction,com.liferay.portal.events.LoginPostAction
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Logout event </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    logout.events.pre=com.liferay.portal.events.LogoutPreAction
    logout.events.post=com.liferay.portal.events.LogoutPostAction,com.liferay.portal.events.DefaultLogoutPageAction,com.liferay.portal.events.SiteMinderLogoutAction
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    logout.events.post=com.liferay.portal.events.LogoutPostAction,com.liferay.portal.events.GarbageCollectorAction
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Default Landing Page"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Default Landing Page</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the default landing page path for logged in users relative to the server path. This is the page users are automatically redirected to after logging in. For example, if you want the default landing page to be http://localhost:8080/web/guest/login, set this to /web/guest/login. To activate this feature, set auth.forward.by.last.path to true. To customize the behavior, see com.liferay.portal.events.DefaultLandingPageAction in the "login.events.post" property above. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    default.landing.page.path=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    default.landing.page.path=/web/guest/login
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Default Logout Page"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Default Logout Page</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the default logout page path for users relative to the server path. This is the page users are automatically redirected to after logging out. For example, if you want the default logout page to be http://localhost:8080/web/guest/logout, set this to /web/guest/logout. To activate this feature, set auth.forward.by.last.path to true. To customize the behavior, see com.liferay.portal.events.DefaultLogoutPageAction in the "logout.events.post" property above. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    default.logout.page.path=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    default.logout.page.path=/web/guest/logout
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Default Guest Public Layouts"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Default Guest Public Layouts</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>The Guest group must have at least one public page. The settings for the initial public page are specified in the following properties. </p> 
  <p>If you need to add more than one page, set the property "default.guest.public.layouts.lar" to specifiy a LAR file instead. </p> 
  <p>For even more complex behavior, override the addDefaultGuestPublicLayouts method in com.liferay.portal.service.impl.GroupLocalServiceImpl. </p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the name of the public layout. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    default.guest.public.layout.name=Welcome
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the layout template id of the public layout. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    default.guest.public.layout.template.id=2_columns_ii
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the portlet ids for the columns specified in the layout template. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    default.guest.public.layout.column-1=58
    default.guest.public.layout.column-2=47
    default.guest.public.layout.column-3=
    default.guest.public.layout.column-4=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the friendly url of the public layout. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    default.guest.public.layout.friendly.url=/home
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the regular theme id for the public layout. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    default.guest.public.layout.regular.theme.id=classic
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the regular color scheme id for the public layout. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    default.guest.public.layout.regular.color.scheme.id=01
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the wap theme id for the public layout. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    default.guest.public.layout.wap.theme.id=mobile
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the wap color scheme for the public layout. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    default.guest.public.layout.wap.color.scheme.id=01
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Specify a LAR file that can be used to create the guest public layouts. If this property is set, the previous layout properties will be ignored. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    default.guest.public.layouts.lar=${liferay.home}/deploy/default_guest_public.lar
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr>

  <hr> 
  <a name="Layouts"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Layouts</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the list of layout types. The display text of each of the layout types is set in content/Language.properties and prefixed with "layout.types.". </p> 
  <p>You can create new layout types and specify custom settings for each layout type. End users input dynamic values as designed in the edit page. End users see the layout as designed in the view page. The generated URL can reference properties set in the edit page. Parentable layouts can contain child layouts. You can also specify a comma delimited list of configuration actions that will be called for your layout when it is updated or deleted. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.types=portlet,panel,embedded,url,link_to_layout
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of sections that will be included as part of the layout form when adding a layout. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.form.add=details
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of sections that will be included as part of the layout form when updating a layout. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.form.update=details,seo,look-and-feel,layout,javascript,custom-fields,advanced,mobile-rule-groups
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of sections that will be included as part of the layout set form when updating a layout set. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.set.form.update=look-and-feel,logo,javascript,advanced,mobile-rule-groups
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set whether or not private layouts are enabled. Set whether or not private layouts should be auto created if a user has no private layouts. If private layouts are not enabled, then the property "layout.user.private.layouts.auto.create" is assumed to be false. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.user.private.layouts.enabled=true
    layout.user.private.layouts.auto.create=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if users must have the Power User role to have private pages. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.user.private.layouts.power.user.required=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set whether or not public layouts are enabled. Set whether or not public layouts should be auto created if a user has no public layouts. If public layouts are not enabled, then the property "layout.user.public.layouts.auto.create" is assumed to be false. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.user.public.layouts.enabled=true
    layout.user.public.layouts.auto.create=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if users must have the Power User role to have public pages. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.user.public.layouts.power.user.required=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Default settings layouts. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.edit.page=/portal/layout/edit/portlet.jsp
    layout.view.page=/portal/layout/view/portlet.jsp
    layout.url=${liferay:mainPath}/portal/layout?p_l_id=${liferay:plid}&amp;p_v_l_s_g_id=${liferay:pvlsgid}
    layout.url.friendliable=true
    layout.parentable=true
    layout.sitemapable=true
    layout.first.pageable=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    layout.configuration.action.update=
    layout.configuration.action.delete=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Settings for portlet layouts are inherited from the default settings. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    layout.edit.page[portlet]=/portal/layout/edit/portlet.jsp
    layout.view.page[portlet]=/portal/layout/view/portlet.jsp
    layout.url[portlet]=${liferay:mainPath}/portal/layout?p_l_id=${liferay:plid}&amp;p_v_l_s_g_id=${liferay:pvlsgid}
    layout.url.friendliable[portlet]=true
    layout.parentable[portlet]=true
    layout.configuration.action.update[portlet]=
    layout.configuration.action.delete[portlet]=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Settings for panel layouts. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.edit.page[panel]=/portal/layout/edit/panel.jsp
    layout.view.page[panel]=/portal/layout/view/panel.jsp
    layout.url[panel]=${liferay:mainPath}/portal/layout?p_l_id=${liferay:plid}&amp;p_v_l_s_g_id=${liferay:pvlsgid}
    layout.url.friendliable[panel]=true
    layout.parentable[panel]=true
    layout.first.pageable[panel]=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Settings for control_panel layouts. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.edit.page[control_panel]=/portal/layout/edit/control_panel.jsp
    layout.view.page[control_panel]=/portal/layout/view/control_panel.jsp
    layout.url[control_panel]=${liferay:mainPath}/portal/layout?p_l_id=${liferay:plid}&amp;p_v_l_s_g_id=${liferay:pvlsgid}
    layout.url.friendliable[control_panel]=true
    layout.parentable[control_panel]=true
    layout.first.pageable[control_panel]=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Settings for embedded layouts. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.edit.page[embedded]=/portal/layout/edit/embedded.jsp
    layout.view.page[embedded]=/portal/layout/view/embedded.jsp
    layout.url[embedded]=${liferay:mainPath}/portal/layout?p_l_id=${liferay:plid}&amp;p_v_l_s_g_id=${liferay:pvlsgid}
    layout.url.friendliable[embedded]=true
    layout.parentable[embedded]=false
    layout.sitemapable[embedded]=true
    layout.first.pageable[embedded]=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    layout.configuration.action.update[embedded]=
    layout.configuration.action.delete[embedded]=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Settings for article layouts. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.edit.page[article]=/portal/layout/edit/article.jsp
    layout.view.page[article]=/portal/layout/view/article.jsp
    layout.url.friendliable[article]=true
    layout.url[article]=${liferay:mainPath}/portal/layout?p_l_id=${liferay:plid}&amp;p_v_l_s_g_id=${liferay:pvlsgid}
    layout.parentable[article]=false
    layout.sitemapable[article]=true
    layout.first.pageable[article]=true
    layout.configuration.action.update[article]=com.liferay.portal.model.LayoutTypeArticleConfigurationUpdateAction
    layout.configuration.action.delete[article]=com.liferay.portal.model.LayoutTypeArticleConfigurationDeleteAction
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Settings for URL layouts. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.edit.page[url]=/portal/layout/edit/url.jsp
    layout.view.page[url]=
    layout.url[url]=${url}
    layout.url.friendliable[url]=true
    layout.parentable[url]=false
    layout.sitemapable[url]=false
    layout.first.pageable[url]=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    layout.configuration.action.update[url]=
    layout.configuration.action.delete[url]=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Settings for page layouts. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.edit.page[link_to_layout]=/portal/layout/edit/link_to_layout.jsp
    layout.view.page[link_to_layout]=
    layout.url[link_to_layout]=${liferay:mainPath}/portal/layout?p_v_l_s_g_id=${liferay:pvlsgid}&amp;groupId=${liferay:groupId}&amp;privateLayout=${privateLayout}&amp;layoutId=${linkToLayoutId}
    layout.url.friendliable[link_to_layout]=true
    layout.parentable[link_to_layout]=true
    layout.sitemapable[link_to_layout]=false
    layout.first.pageable[link_to_layout]=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    layout.configuration.action.update[link_to_layout]=
    layout.configuration.action.delete[link_to_layout]=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Specify static portlets that cannot be moved and will always appear on every layout. Static portlets will take precedence over portlets that may have been dynamically configured for the layout. </p> 
  <p>For example, if you want the Hello World portlet to always appear at the start of the iteration of the first column for user layouts, set the property "layout.static.portlets.start.column-1[user]" to "47". If you want the Hello World portlet to always appear at the end of the second column for user layouts, set the property "layout.static.portlets.end.column-2[user]" to "47". You can input a list of comma delimited portlet ids to specify more than one portlet. If the portlet is instanceable, add the suffix "_INSTANCE_abcd" to the portlet id, where "abcd" is any random alphanumeric string. </p> 
  <p>The static portlets are fetched based on the properties controlled by custom filters using EasyConf. By default, the available filters are user, community, and organization. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    layout.static.portlets.start.column-1[user]=3,6
    layout.static.portlets.end.column-1[user]=14
    layout.static.portlets.start.column-2[user]=71_INSTANCE_abcd,7
    layout.static.portlets.end.column-2[user]=34,70
    layout.static.portlets.start.column-3[user]=
    layout.static.portlets.end.column-3[user]=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>It is also possible to set static portlets based on the layout's friendly URL. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    layout.static.portlets.start.column-1[user][/home]=3,6
    layout.static.portlets.end.column-2[regular-site][/home]=14
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the static portlets for the pages of regular sites. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    layout.static.portlets.start.column-1[regular-site]=
    layout.static.portlets.end.column-1[regular-site]=
    layout.static.portlets.start.column-2[regular-site]=
    layout.static.portlets.end.column-2[regular-site]=
    layout.static.portlets.start.column-3[regular-site]=
    layout.static.portlets.end.column-3[regular-site]=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the static portlets for the pages of organization sites. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    layout.static.portlets.start.column-1[organization]=
    layout.static.portlets.end.column-1[organization]=
    layout.static.portlets.start.column-2[organization]=
    layout.static.portlets.end.column-2[organization]=
    layout.static.portlets.start.column-3[organization]=
    layout.static.portlets.end.column-3[organization]=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the static portlets that will appear for every layout. See /html/portal/layout/view/common.jspf for the logic of when these portlets will be shown. For example, these portlets will only show for layouts that can contain portlets and are not in a pop up state. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.static.portlets.all=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the private group, private user, and public servlet mapping for com.liferay.portal.servlet.FriendlyURLServlet. This value must match the servlet mapping set in web.xml. </p> 
  <p>For example, if the private group pages are mapped to "/group" and the group's friendly URL is set to "/guest" and the layout's friendly URL is set to "/company/community", then the friendly URL for the page will be http://www.liferay.com/group/guest/company/community. Private group pages map to a site's private pages and are only available to authenticated users with the proper permissions. </p> 
  <p>For example, if the public pages are mapped to "/web" and the group or user's friendly URL is set to "/guest" and the layout's friendly URL is set to "/company/community", then the friendly URL for the page will be http://www.liferay.com/web/guest/company/community. Public pages are available to unauthenticated users. </p> 
  <p>The friendly URL's for users, groups, and layouts can be set during runtime. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.friendly.url.private.group.servlet.mapping=/group
    layout.friendly.url.private.user.servlet.mapping=/user
    layout.friendly.url.public.servlet.mapping=/web
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Redirect to this resource if the user requested a friendly URL that does not exist. Leave it blank to display nothing. </p> 
  <p>Note: For backward compatibility, this overrides the property "layout.show.http.status" for the 404 status code. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    layout.friendly.url.page.not.found=/html/portal/404.html
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the reserved keywords that cannot be used in a friendly URL. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.friendly.url.keywords=\
        _vti_*,\
        api*,\
        c,\
        combo,\
        delegate,\
        display_chart*,\
        dtd,\
        elqNow,\
        facebook,\
        google_gadget,\
        group,\
        html,\
        image,\
        language,\
        lucene,\
        netvibes,\
        osgi,\
        page,\
        pbhs,\
        poller,\
        private,\
        public,\
        rest,\
        robots.txt,\
        sharepoint*,\
        sitemap.xml,\
        software_catalog*,\
        tunnel-web,\
        wap,\
        web,\
        webdav*,\
        widget,\
        xmlrpc
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if guest users should see the maximize window icon. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.guest.show.max.icon=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if guest users should see the minimize window icon. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.guest.show.min.icon=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if users are shown that they do not have access to a portlet. The portlet init parameter "show-portlet-access-denied" will override this setting. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.show.portlet.access.denied=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if users are shown that a portlet is inactive. The portlet init parameter "show-portlet-inactive" will override this setting. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.show.portlet.inactive=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if the portal should show HTTP status codes like 404 if the requested page is not found. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.show.http.status=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the default layout template id used when creating layouts. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.default.template.id=2_columns_ii
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to false to disable parallel rendering. You can also disable it on a per request basis by setting the attribute key com.liferay.portal.util.WebKeys.PORTLET_PARALLEL_RENDER to the Boolean.FALSE in a pre service event or by setting the URL parameter "p_p_parallel" to "0". </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.parallel.render.enable=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the name of a class that implements com.liferay.portal.util.LayoutClone. This class is used to remember maximized and minimized states on shared pages. The default implementation persists the state in the browser session. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.clone.impl=com.liferay.portal.util.SessionLayoutClone
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to cache the content of layout templates. This is recommended because it improves performance for production servers. Setting it to false is useful during development if you need to make a lot of changes. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.template.cache.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the default value for the "p_l_reset" parameter. If set to true, then render parameters are cleared when different pages are hit. This is not the behavior promoted by the portlet specification, but is the one that most end users seem to prefer. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.default.p_l_reset=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable comments for pages. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.comments.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to remember maximized window states across different pages. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.remember.maximized.window.state=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to specify the initial number of child pages to display in the Manage Pages tree. Set this to -1 to show all. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    layout.manage.pages.initial.children=20
</pre>

  <a name="Layout Prototypes"></a>

  <p>Set this property to true to enable the propagation of changes to a page from its page template by default. </p>

  <pre class="defaults">    layout.prototype.link.enabled.default=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>In the case that a page template would fail to merge, make sure that we prevent repeated attempts that will inevitably fail by having a fail threshold. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em>

  <pre class="defaults">    layout.prototype.merge.fail.threshold=3
</pre>
  <p></p>

  <hr> 
  <a name="Portlet URL"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Portlet URL</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if calling setParameter on a portlet URL appends the parameter value versus replacing it. There is some disagreement in the interpretation of the JSR 168 spec among portlet developers over this specific behavior. Liferay Portal successfully passes the portlet TCK tests whether this value is set to true or false. </p> 
  <p>See http://issues.liferay.com/browse/LEP-426 for more information. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    portlet.url.append.parameters=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to allow portlet URLs to generate with an anchor tag. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    portlet.url.anchor.enable=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>JSR 286 specifies that portlet URLs are escaped by default. Set this to false to provide for better backwards compatibility. </p> 
  <p>If this is set to true, but a specific portlet application requires that its portlet URLs not be escaped by default, then modify portlet.xml and set the container runtime option "javax.portlet.escapeXml" to false. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    portlet.url.escape.xml=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set a list of comma delimited reserved parameters that will not be added to refresh URL. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    portlet.url.refresh.url.reserved.parameters=password,password1,password2,pop3Password,properties--jdbc.default.password,settings--google.apps.password,smtpPassword,settings--ldap.security.credentials
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Preferences"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Preferences</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to validate portlet preferences on startup. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    preference.validate.on.startup=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Redirect"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Redirect</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this property to "ip" or "domain" for the redirect security method. If set to "domain", the portal will only redirect users to domains listed in the property "redirect.url.domain.allowed". If set to "ip", the portal will only redirect to domains whose IP address resolve to an IP address listed in the property "redirect.url.ip.allowed". </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    redirect.url.security.mode=ip
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    redirect.url.security.mode=domain
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited domains which the portal is allowed to redirect to. Input a blank list to allow any domain. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    redirect.url.domains.allowed=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited IPs which the portal is allowed to redirect to. Input a blank list to allow any IP. SERVER_IP will be replaced with the IP of the host server. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    redirect.url.ips.allowed=127.0.0.1,SERVER_IP
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Struts"></a>

  <a name="Images"></a>

  <h3>Images</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if the Image servlet will automatically scale an image based on the request "height" and "width" parameters. </p>

</pre>
  <p></p>

  <em>Defaults:</em>

</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the location of the default organization logo image that is used for missing organization logo images. This image must be available in the class path. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    image.default.organization.logo=com/liferay/portal/dependencies/organization_logo.png
</pre>
  <p></p>

  <pre class="defaults">    image.default.user.female.portrait=com/liferay/portal/dependencies/user_female_portrait.png
    image.default.user.male.portrait=com/liferay/portal/dependencies/user_male_portrait.png
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>In versions prior to 6.1, the Image Gallery portlet supported persisting images via com.liferay.portal.image.DatabaseHook, com.liferay.portal.image.DLHook, or com.liferay.portal.image.FileSystemHook. Since 6.1, only DLHook is supported. </p> 
  <p>Set this property to the hook implementation to trigger automatic data migration during an upgrade. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    image.hook.impl=com.liferay.portal.image.DatabaseHook
    image.hook.impl=com.liferay.portal.image.DLHook
    image.hook.impl=com.liferay.portal.image.FileSystemHook
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>This is a legacy property used by the FileSystemHook to allow data migration from other hooks. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    image.hook.file.system.root.dir=${liferay.home}/data/images
</pre>
  <p></p>

  <a name="Fields"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Fields</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the following fields to false so users cannot see them. Some company policies require gender and birthday information to always be hidden. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    field.enable.com.liferay.portal.model.Contact.male=true
    field.enable.com.liferay.portal.model.Contact.birthday=true
    field.enable.com.liferay.portal.model.Organization.status=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited user types who can edit their own fields. Valid types are "administrator", "user-with-mx", and "user-without-mx". </p> 
  <p>Set a value of "administrator" if an administrator can edit the specified field. An administrator is anyone who has the Administrator role. </p> 
  <p>Set a value of "user-with-mx" if a user who has an email address that matches the company mail suffix can edit the specified field. </p> 
  <p>Set a value of "user-without-mx" if a user who does not have an email address that matches the company mail suffix can edit the specified field. </p> 
  <p>Set all three values if all users can edit the specified field. Set a combination of the three values if only a combination of the users can edit the specified field. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    field.editable.com.liferay.portal.model.User.screenName=administrator,user-with-mx,user-without-mx
    field.editable.com.liferay.portal.model.User.emailAddress=administrator,user-with-mx,user-without-mx
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr>

  <a name="Browser Cache"></a>

  <h3>Browser Cache</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if you want the portal to force the browser cache to be disabled. It will only disable the cache for the rendered HTML response. It will not have an impact on static content or other resources. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    browser.cache.disabled=false
</pre>
  <p></p>

  <p>Set this true if you want to disable the cache for authenticated users. This property is not read when the property "browser.cache.signed.in.disabled" is true. This is useful to ensure that authenticated users cannot go to the sign in page by clicking on the back button in their browsers. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    browser.cache.signed.in.disabled=false
</pre>

  <a name="Instant Messenger"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Instant Messenger</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the AIM login and password by which the system will use AIM to communicate with users. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    aim.login=
    aim.password=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Due to a bug in JOscarLib 0.3b1, you must set the full path to the ICQ jar. </p> 
  <p>See the following posts: </p> 
  <p></p>
  <pre>     http://sourceforge.net/projects/ooimlib/forums/forum/166562/topic/843299?message=1972697
     http://sourceforge.net/projects/ooimlib/forums/forum/166562/topic/843299?message=1990487
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    icq.jar=C:/Java/orion-2.0.7/lib/icq.jar
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the ICQ login and password by which the system will use ICQ to communicate with users. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    icq.login=
    icq.password=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the MSN login and password by which the system will use MSN to communicate with users. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    msn.login=
    msn.password=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the YM login and password by which the system will use YM to communicate with users. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    ym.login=
    ym.password=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Lucene Search"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Lucene Search</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable highlighting of search results. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.search.highlight.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the fragment size returned from the search result highlighter </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.search.highlight.fragment.size=80
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the number of lines for the snippet returned by search engine. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.search.highlight.snippet.size=3
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the limit for results used when performing index searches. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.search.limit=10000
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable scoring of results </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.search.scoring.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the search engine for each indexer implementation by assigning the search engine id. The search engine ids are defined in the spring configuration files. The default engine id is SYSTEM_ENGINE and will be used as the default for all indexers unless configured to use something else. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    index.search.engine.id[com.liferay.portlet.journal.util.JournalIndexer]=SYSTEM_ENGINE
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the limit for results used when performing index searches that are subsequently filtered by permissions. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.filter.search.limit=5000
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if you want to avoid any writes to the index. This is useful in some clustering environments where there is a shared index and only one node of the cluster updates it. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.read.only=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if you want to index your entire library of files on startup. This property is available so that automated test environments index on startup. Do not set this to true on production systems or else your index will be indexed on every startup. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.on.startup=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to add a delay before indexing on startup. A delay may be necessary if a lot of plugins need to be loaded and reindexed. This property is only valid if "index.on.startup" is set to true. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.on.startup.delay=60
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if you want to index your entire library of files after an upgrade. Only set this property to false if you are running a small upgrade and you do not need to reindex everything. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.on.upgrade=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if you want the indexing on startup to be executed on a separate thread to speed up execution. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.with.thread=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the date format used for storing dates as text in the index. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.date.format.pattern=yyyyMMddHHmmss
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if you want to use compress index files before they are dumped. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.dump.compression.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Enter a list of comma delimited field names that will be copied to an untokenized field for sorting. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.sortable.text.fields=firstName,jobTitle,lastName,name,screenName,title
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the maximum length for sortable keyword fields before they are truncated. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    index.sortable.text.fields.truncated.length=255
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the maximum number of clauses to allow in a boolean query. The default is 1024. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    lucene.boolean.query.clause.max.size=1024
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Designate whether Lucene stores indexes in a file system or in RAM. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    lucene.store.type=file
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    lucene.store.type=ram
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>When using file store, turning this flag on will tell Lucene to use MMapDirectory rather than using the default selection (SimpleFSDirectory for Windows and NIOFSDirectory for Linux). It only makes sense to use MMapDirectory for 64-bit JVM with a lot of memory. On a 32-bit JVM, if the index files are huge, this could easily lead to an out of memory for non-heap memory. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    lucene.store.type.file.force.mmap=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the directory where Lucene indexes are stored. This is only referenced if Lucene stores indexes in the file system. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    lucene.dir=${liferay.home}/data/lucene/
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a class name that extends com.liferay.portal.search.lucene.LuceneFileExtractor. This class is called by Lucene to extract text from complex files so that they can be properly indexed. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    lucene.file.extractor=com.liferay.portal.search.lucene.LuceneFileExtractor
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>The file extractor can sometimes return text that is not valid for Lucene. This property expects a regular expression. Any character that does not matche the regular expression will be replaced with a blank space. Set an empty regular expression to disable this feature. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    lucene.file.extractor.regexp.strip=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    lucene.file.extractor.regexp.strip=[\\d\\w]
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set how often index updates will be committed. Set the batch size to configure how many consecutive updates will trigger a commit. If the value is 0, then the index will be committed on every update. Set the time interval in milliseconds to configure how often to commit the index. The time interval is not read unless the batch size is greater than 0 because the time interval works in conjunction with the batch size to guarantee that the index is committed after a specified time interval. Set the time interval to 0 to disable committing the index by a time interval. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    lucene.commit.batch.size=0
    lucene.commit.time.interval=0
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the maximum number of tokens generated by the analyzer while indexing. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    lucene.analyzer.max.tokens=10000
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set Lucene's buffer size in megabytes. Higher numbers mean indexing goes faster but uses more memory. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    lucene.buffer.size=16
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set Lucene's merge factor. Higher numbers mean indexing goes faster but uses more memory. The default value from Lucene is 10. This should never be set to a number lower than 2. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    lucene.merge.factor=10
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a class name that extends org.apache.lucene.index.MergePolicy. Lucene uses this class to determine the sequence of primitive merge operations. Note that the property "lucene.merge.factor" is not only used by LogDocMergePolicy. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    lucene.merge.policy=org.apache.lucene.index.LogDocMergePolicy
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    lucene.merge.policy=org.apache.lucene.index.LogByteSizeMergePolicy
    lucene.merge.policy=org.apache.lucene.index.NoMergePolicy
    lucene.merge.policy=org.apache.lucene.index.TieredMergePolicy
    lucene.merge.policy=org.apache.lucene.index.UpgradeIndexMergePolicy
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if you want the portal to replicate an index write across all members of the cluster. This is useful in some clustered environments where you wish each server instance to have its own copy of the Lucene search index. This is only relevant when using the default Lucene indexing engine. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    lucene.replicate.write=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Specify the Lucene cluster index loading synchronization timeout in milliseconds. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    lucene.cluster.index.loading.sync.timeout=60000
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Multi Value Map"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Multi Value Map</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the multi value map property to 0 to store the map in memory and 1 to store the map in the file system. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    multi.value.map.com.liferay.portal.convert.ConvertPermissionAlgorithm.convertResourcePermission=0
    multi.value.map.com.liferay.portal.convert.ConvertPermissionAlgorithm.convertRoles=0
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Setup Wizard"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Setup Wizard</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set a comma delimited list of supported databases. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    setup.database.types=db2,derby,hypersonic,ingres,mysql,oracle,postgresql,sqlserver,sybase
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    setup.database.driverClassName[db2]=com.ibm.db2.jcc.DB2Driver
    setup.database.driverClassName[derby]=org.apache.derby.jdbc.EmbeddedDriver
    setup.database.driverClassName[hypersonic]=org.hsqldb.jdbcDriver
    setup.database.driverClassName[ingres]=com.ingres.jdbc.IngresDriver
    setup.database.driverClassName[mysql]=com.mysql.jdbc.Driver
    setup.database.driverClassName[oracle]=oracle.jdbc.driver.OracleDriver
    setup.database.driverClassName[postgresql]=org.postgresql.Driver
    setup.database.driverClassName[sqlserver]=net.sourceforge.jtds.jdbc.Driver
    setup.database.driverClassName[sybase]=net.sourceforge.jtds.jdbc.Driver
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    setup.database.jar.name[com.mysql.jdbc.Driver]=mysql.jar
    setup.database.jar.url[com.mysql.jdbc.Driver]=http://repo1.maven.org/maven2/mysql/mysql-connector-java/5.1.23/mysql-connector-java-5.1.23.jar
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    setup.database.url[db2]=jdbc:db2://localhost:50000/lportal:deferPrepares=false;fullyMaterializeInputStreams=true;fullyMaterializeLobData=true;progresssiveLocators=2;progressiveStreaming=2;
    setup.database.url[derby]=jdbc:derby:lportal
    setup.database.url[hypersonic]=jdbc:hsqldb:${liferay.home}/data/hsql/lportal
    setup.database.url[ingres]=jdbc:ingres://localhost:II7/lportal
    setup.database.url[mysql]=jdbc:mysql://localhost/lportal?useUnicode=true&amp;characterEncoding=UTF-8&amp;useFastDateParsing=false
    setup.database.url[oracle]=jdbc:oracle:thin:@localhost:1521:xe
    setup.database.url[postgresql]=jdbc:postgresql://localhost:5432/lportal
    setup.database.url[sqlserver]=jdbc:jtds:sqlserver://localhost/lportal
    setup.database.url[sybase]=jdbc:jtds:sybase://localhost:5000/lportal
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this property to true if the Setup Wizard should be displayed the first the portal is started. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    setup.wizard.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p>

  <hr> 
  <a name="Value Object"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Value Object</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>You can add a listener for a specific class by setting the property "value.object.listener" with a list of comma delimited class names that implement com.liferay.portal.model.ModelListener. These classes are pooled and reused and must be thread safe. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    value.object.listener.com.liferay.portal.model.Contact=com.liferay.portal.model.ContactListener
    value.object.listener.com.liferay.portal.model.Layout=com.liferay.portal.model.LayoutListener,com.liferay.portal.service.impl.LayoutSetPrototypeLayoutListener
    value.object.listener.com.liferay.portal.model.LayoutSet=com.liferay.portal.model.LayoutSetListener,com.liferay.portal.service.impl.LayoutSetPrototypeLayoutSetListener
    value.object.listener.com.liferay.portal.model.PortletPreferences=com.liferay.portal.model.PortletPreferencesListener
    value.object.listener.com.liferay.portal.model.User=com.liferay.portal.model.UserListener
    value.object.listener.com.liferay.portal.model.UserGroup=com.liferay.portal.model.UserGroupListener
    value.object.listener.com.liferay.portlet.journal.model.JournalArticle=com.liferay.portlet.journal.model.JournalArticleListener
    value.object.listener.com.liferay.portlet.journal.model.JournalTemplate=com.liferay.portlet.journal.model.JournalTemplateListener
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Value objects are cached at three levels. They first level is "entity", the second level is "finder", and the third level is "Hibernate". </p> 
  <p>The entity level cache stores a value object's primary key to the value object itself. </p> 
  <p>The finder level cache stores the many paths that return a value object and the many paths that return a list of value objects. The finder level cache only caches primary keys and is further helped by the entity level cache that caches the value object to the primary key. </p> 
  <p>The Hibernate level cache is provided by the "hibernate.cache.provider_class" property. </p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable entity level caching. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    value.object.entity.cache.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to configure entity level caching to block. See the property "ehcache.blocking.cache.allowed" for more information. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    value.object.entity.blocking.cache=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>The entity level cache uses a thread local map to store the most frequently accessed items to lower the number of queries to the underlying cache. Set the maximum map size to 0 to disable the thread level cache. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    value.object.entity.thread.local.cache.max.size=100
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Entity level caching for a specific type of value object can be configured by using a property name that includes the value object's class name. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    value.object.entity.cache.enabled.com.liferay.portal.model.Layout=true
    value.object.entity.cache.enabled.com.liferay.portal.model.User=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable finder level caching. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    value.object.finder.cache.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to configure finder level caching to block. See the property "ehcache.blocking.cache.allowed" for more information. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    value.object.finder.blocking.cache=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>The finder level cache uses a thread local map to store the most frequently accessed items to lower the number of queries to the underlying cache. Set the maximum map size to 0 to disable the thread level cache. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    value.object.finder.thread.local.cache.max.size=100
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Finder level caching for a specific type of value object can be configured by using a property name that includes the value object's class name. Mapping tables can also be specified to configure the caching of value object relationships. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    value.object.finder.cache.enabled.com.liferay.portal.model.Layout=true
    value.object.finder.cache.enabled.com.liferay.portal.model.User=true
    value.object.finder.cache.enabled.Users_Roles=true
</pre>
  <p></p>
