</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the location of the default content for each language type. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    journal.template.language.content[css]=com/liferay/portlet/journal/dependencies/template.css
    journal.template.language.content[ftl]=com/liferay/portlet/journal/dependencies/template.ftl
    journal.template.language.content[vm]=com/liferay/portlet/journal/dependencies/template.vm
    journal.template.language.content[xsl]=com/liferay/portlet/journal/dependencies/template.xsl
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the parser for each language type. A parser is only needed for language types that require parsing. The classes must implement com.liferay.portal.kernel.templateparser.TemplateParser. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    journal.template.language.parser[css]=
    journal.template.language.parser[ftl]=com.liferay.portlet.journal.util.FreeMarkerTemplateParser
    journal.template.language.parser[vm]=com.liferay.portlet.journal.util.VelocityTemplateParser
    journal.template.language.parser[xsl]=com.liferay.portlet.journal.util.XSLTemplateParser
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a comma delimited list of variables which are restricted from the context in FreeMarker based Journal templates. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    journal.template.freemarker.restricted.variables=serviceLocator
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a comma delimited list of variables which are restricted from the context in Velocity based Journal templates. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    journal.template.velocity.restricted.variables=serviceLocator
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the maximum file size and valid file extensions for images. A value of 0 for the maximum file size can be used to indicate unlimited file size. However, the maximum file size allowed is set in the property "com.liferay.portal.upload.UploadServletRequestImpl.max.size". </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    journal.image.small.max.size=51200
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>A file extension of * will permit all file extensions. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    journal.image.extensions=.gif,.jpeg,.jpg,.png
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of comma delimited class names that extend com.liferay.portal.kernel.templateparser.BaseTransformerListener. These classes will run in sequence to allow you to modify the XML and XSL before it is transformed and allow you to modify the final output. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    journal.transformer.listener=\
        com.liferay.portlet.journal.util.TokensTransformerListener,\
        #com.liferay.portlet.journal.util.PropertiesTransformerListener,\
        com.liferay.portlet.journal.util.ContentTransformerListener,\
        com.liferay.portlet.journal.util.LocaleTransformerListener,\
        com.liferay.portlet.journal.util.RegexTransformerListener,\
        com.liferay.portlet.journal.util.ViewCounterTransformerListener
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Enter a list of regular expression patterns and replacements that will be applied to outputted Journal content. The list of properties must end with a subsequent integer (0, 1, etc.) and it is assumed that the list has reached an end when the pattern or replacement is not set. See com.liferay.portlet.journal.util.RegexTransformerListener for implementation details. </p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    journal.transformer.regex.pattern.0=beta.sample.com
    journal.transformer.regex.replacement.0=production.sample.com
    journal.transformer.regex.pattern.1=staging.sample.com
    journal.transformer.regex.replacement.1=production.sample.com
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if journal articles should be published to live by default. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    journal.publish.to.live.by.default=true
</pre>
  <p></p>

  <hr> 
  <a name="Ratings Tag Library"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Ratings Tag Library</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the number of stars that will be used by the ratings tag library by default. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    ratings.default.number.of.stars=5
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the number of max score and min score that will be used by the ratings tag library for each model. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    ratings.max.score[com.liferay.portlet.messageboards.model.MBDiscussion]=1
    ratings.min.score[com.liferay.portlet.messageboards.model.MBDiscussion]=-1
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    ratings.max.score[com.liferay.portlet.messageboards.model.MBMessage]=1
    ratings.min.score[com.liferay.portlet.messageboards.model.MBMessage]=-1
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="RSS Portlet"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>RSS Portlet</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the HTTP connection timeout in milliseconds for reading RSS feeds. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    rss.connection.timeout=2000
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Search Portlet"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Search Portlet</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set any of these to false to disable the portlet from being searched by the Search portlet. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    com.liferay.portlet.blogs.util.BlogsOpenSearchImpl=true
    com.liferay.portlet.bookmarks.util.BookmarksOpenSearchImpl=true
    com.liferay.portlet.calendar.util.CalendarOpenSearchImpl=true
    com.liferay.portlet.directory.util.DirectoryOpenSearchImpl=true
    com.liferay.portlet.documentlibrary.util.DLOpenSearchImpl=true
    com.liferay.portlet.journal.util.JournalOpenSearchImpl=true
    com.liferay.portlet.messageboards.util.MBOpenSearchImpl=true
    com.liferay.portlet.wiki.util.WikiOpenSearchImpl=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Sites Admin Portlet"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Sites Admin Portlet</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to allow site members to see the Sites Admin portlet and the sites he is a member of in the Control Panel. Setting this to false will only allow administrators to see this portlet in the Control Panel. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    sites.control.panel.members.visible=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of sections that will be included as part of the form when adding a site. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    sites.form.add.main=details,categorization
    sites.form.add.seo=
    sites.form.add.advanced=
    sites.form.add.miscellaneous=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Input a list of sections that will be included as part of the form when updating a site. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    sites.form.update.main=details,categorization,site-url,site-template
    sites.form.update.seo=sitemap,robots
    sites.form.update.advanced=staging,analytics
    sites.form.update.miscellaneous=custom-fields
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Configure email notification settings. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    sites.email.from.name=
    sites.email.from.address=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    sites.email.membership.reply.subject=com/liferay/portlet/sites/dependencies/email_membership_reply_subject.tmpl
    sites.email.membership.reply.body=com/liferay/portlet/sites/dependencies/email_membership_reply_body.tmpl
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    sites.email.membership.request.subject=com/liferay/portlet/sites/dependencies/email_membership_request_subject.tmpl
    sites.email.membership.request.body=com/liferay/portlet/sites/dependencies/email_membership_request_body.tmpl
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the default change frequency for pages. This change frequency value will be used by the robots visiting the pages. Possible values are: always, hourly, daily, weekly, monthly, yearly, or never. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    sites.sitemap.default.change.frequency=daily
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the default priority for pages. This priority value will used by the robots visiting the pages. The possible value range is 0.0 to 1.0. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    sites.sitemap.default.priority=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Shopping Portlet"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Shopping Portlet</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true if cart quantities must be a multiple of the item's minimum quantity. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    shopping.cart.min.qty.multiple=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to forward to the cart page when adding an item from the category page. The item must not have dynamic fields. All items with dynamic fields will forward to the item's details page regardless of the following setting. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    shopping.category.forward.to.cart=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to show special items when browsing a category. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    shopping.category.show.special.items=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to show availability when viewing an item. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    shopping.item.show.availability=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the maximum file size and valid file extensions for images. A value of 0 for the maximum file size can be used to indicate unlimited file size. However, the maximum file size allowed is set in the property "com.liferay.portal.upload.UploadServletRequestImpl.max.size". </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    shopping.image.small.max.size=51200
    shopping.image.medium.max.size=153600
    shopping.image.large.max.size=307200
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>A file extension of * will permit all file extensions. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    shopping.image.extensions=.gif,.jpeg,.jpg,.png
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Configure email notification settings. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    shopping.email.from.name=
    shopping.email.from.address=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    shopping.email.order.confirmation.enabled=true
    shopping.email.order.confirmation.subject=com/liferay/portlet/shopping/dependencies/email_order_confirmation_subject.tmpl
    shopping.email.order.confirmation.body=com/liferay/portlet/shopping/dependencies/email_order_confirmation_body.tmpl
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    shopping.email.order.shipping.enabled=true
    shopping.email.order.shipping.subject=com/liferay/portlet/shopping/dependencies/email_order_shipping_subject.tmpl
    shopping.email.order.shipping.body=com/liferay/portlet/shopping/dependencies/email_order_shipping_body.tmpl
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable comments for shopping orders. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    shopping.order.comments.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Software Catalog Portlet"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Software Catalog Portlet</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the maximum file size and dimensions for thumbnnails. A value of 0 for the maximum file size can be used to indicate unlimited file size. However, the maximum file size allowed is set in the property "com.liferay.portal.upload.UploadServletRequestImpl.max.size". </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    sc.image.max.size=307200
    sc.image.thumbnail.max.height=200
    sc.image.thumbnail.max.width=160
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable comments for software catalog products. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    sc.product.comments.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Tags Compiler Portlet"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Tags Compiler Portlet</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable the ability to compile tags from the URL. Disabling it can speed up performance. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    tags.compiler.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Translator Portlet"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Translator Portlet</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the default languages to translate a given text. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    translator.default.languages=en_es
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <a name="Wiki Portlet"></a>
  <a href="portal.properties.html">Top of Page</a> 
  <h3>Wiki Portlet</h3> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the name of the default page for a wiki node. The name for the default page must be a valid wiki word. A wiki word follows the format of having an upper case letter followed by a series of lower case letters followed by another upper case letter and another series of lower case letters. See http://www.usemod.com/cgi-bin/wiki.pl?WhatIsaWiki for more information on wiki naming conventions. It is </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.front.page.name=FrontPage
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the name of the default node that will be automatically created when the Wiki portlet is first used in a site. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.initial.node.name=Main
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Specify the requirements for the names of wiki pages. By default only a few characters are forbidden. Uncomment the regular expression below to allow only CamelCase titles. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.page.titles.regexp=([^\\\\\\[\\]\\|:;%&lt;&gt;]+)
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    wiki.page.titles.regexp=(((\\p{Lu}\\p{Ll}+)_?)+)
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Specify the characters that will be automatically removed from the titles when importing wiki pages. This regexp should remove any characters that are forbidden in the regexp specified in the property "wiki.page.titles.regexp". </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.page.titles.remove.regexp=([\\\\\\[\\]\\|:;%&lt;&gt;]+)
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable ratings for wiki pages. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.page.ratings.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable comments for wiki pages. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.page.comments.enabled=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable social activity notifications on minor edits of a wiki page. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.page.minor.edit.add.social.activity=true
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set this to true to enable email notifications on minor edits of a wiki page. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.page.minor.edit.send.email=false
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the list of supported wiki formats and the default wiki format. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.formats=creole,html,mediawiki
    wiki.formats.default=creole
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Configure settings for each of the wiki formats. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.formats.engine[creole]=com.liferay.portlet.wiki.engines.antlrwiki.CreoleWikiEngine
    wiki.formats.configuration.main[creole]=jspwiki.properties
    wiki.formats.edit.page[creole]=/html/portlet/wiki/edit/wiki.jsp
    wiki.formats.help.page[creole]=/html/portlet/wiki/help/creole.jsp
    wiki.formats.help.url[creole]=http://www.wikicreole.org/wiki/Creole1.0
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Examples:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="examples">    wiki.formats.engine[creole]=com.liferay.portlet.wiki.engines.jspwiki.JSPWikiEngine
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.formats.engine[html]=com.liferay.portlet.wiki.engines.HtmlEngine
    wiki.formats.edit.page[html]=/html/portlet/wiki/edit/html.jsp
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.formats.engine[mediawiki]=com.liferay.portlet.wiki.engines.mediawiki.MediaWikiEngine
    wiki.formats.edit.page[mediawiki]=/html/portlet/wiki/edit/wiki.jsp
    wiki.formats.help.page[mediawiki]=/html/portlet/wiki/help/mediawiki.jsp
    wiki.formats.help.url[mediawiki]=http://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Help:Formatting
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.formats.engine[plain_text]=com.liferay.portlet.wiki.engines.TextEngine
    wiki.formats.edit.page[plain_text]=/html/portlet/wiki/edit/plain_text.jsp
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Set the list of supported wiki importers. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.importers=MediaWiki
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Configure settings for each of the wiki importers. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.importers.page[MediaWiki]=/html/portlet/wiki/import/mediawiki.jsp
    wiki.importers.class[MediaWiki]=com.liferay.portlet.wiki.importers.mediawiki.MediaWikiImporter
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <hr> 
  <p>Configure email notification settings. </p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.email.from.name=
    wiki.email.from.address=
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.email.page.added.enabled=true
    wiki.email.page.added.subject.prefix=com/liferay/portlet/wiki/dependencies/email_page_added_subject_prefix.tmpl
    wiki.email.page.added.body=com/liferay/portlet/wiki/dependencies/email_page_added_body.tmpl
    wiki.email.page.added.signature=com/liferay/portlet/wiki/dependencies/email_page_added_signature.tmpl
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.email.page.updated.enabled=true
    wiki.email.page.updated.subject.prefix=com/liferay/portlet/wiki/dependencies/email_page_updated_subject_prefix.tmpl
    wiki.email.page.updated.body=com/liferay/portlet/wiki/dependencies/email_page_updated_body.tmpl
    wiki.email.page.updated.signature=com/liferay/portlet/wiki/dependencies/email_page_updated_signature.tmpl
</pre>
  <p></p> 
  <em>Defaults:</em> 
  <p></p>
  <pre class="defaults">    wiki.rss.abstract.length=200
</pre>
  <p></p>
